        *>   Handles to file DBIs, Parent, Resource etc....

        01 cthandle                     pic x(4) comp-5.
           88 ClientsHandle             value 1.
           88 DefaultsHandle            value 2.
           88 DescripsHandle            value 3.
           88 DesktopHandle             value 4.
           88 MaterialsHandle           value 5.
           88 ParentHandle              value 6.
           88 ProbesHandle              value 7.
           88 ResourceHandle            value 8.
           88 TechniciansHandle         value 9.
           88 SqlConnectionHandle       value 10.
           88 DateTimeHandle            value 11.

        01 FacilityHandle               pic x(4) comp-5.
           88 GroupsHandle              value 1.
           88 InspectionsHandle         value 2.
           88 ItemsHandle               value 3.
           88 RangesHandle              value 4.
           88 ReadingsHandle            value 5.
           88 SummariesHandle           value 6.
           88 VesselsHandle             value 7.

*------------------------------------------------------------------------

        01 ls-handles.
           05 Object1                     object reference.
           05 Object2                     object reference.

        Procedure Division.

         *> This is an edited version of the copyfile
         *> gethandl.cpy, leaving in only relevant files

         *>-------- general handles


**** NOTE here how I am invoking "backwards" - my main Class is os-App 
which by menu selection invoked this class - now Program B is going back 
to Program-A to get necessary handles. The point being - for each menu 
invocation it's a simple "Invoke this Class". The code for each class 
knows which files/tables or other objects it needs and if they are part 
of the common table held in os-App they can be retrieved as necessasry 
by object reference.


           set DescripsHandle  to true
               invoke os-App "getGeneralHandles"
                 using CtHandle returning ls-handles
                       set os-DescripsDBI to Object1
                       set os-DesTable    to Object2

           set ParentHandle to true
               invoke os-App "getGeneralHandles"
                 using CtHandle returning ls-handles
                       set os-Parent to Object1

           set ResourceHandle  to true
               invoke os-App "getGeneralHandles"
                 using CtHandle returning ls-handles
                       set os-Resource to Object1

         *>-------- facility handles

        End Method "getHandles".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "HelpFromMenu".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
         invoke CtHelp "helpFile" using os-Parent
        End Method "HelpFromMenu".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "initDescripsCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        copy "deslist.cpy"    replacing ==(tag)== by ==ls==.

         initialize                ws-CollectionParams
         compute ws-DataLength   = function length (Des-Name)
         compute ws-Keylength    = function length (Des-Code)
         compute ws-RecordLength = function length (ls-DesListRecord)
         set ofReferences          to true
         move zeroes               to ws-sequence
         move 50                   to ws-Size
         set TypeSorted            to true

        End Method "initDescripsCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "initTitleAndLength".
        *>-----------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 ws-WindowTitle  pic x(18) value "Description Codes ".
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-DialogTitle            pic x(100).
        01 ls-length                 pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-string                 object reference.
        01 ls-temp                   pic x(40).

        Procedure Division.

         move rt-Title (ws-CurrentRectype) to ls-temp
         string ws-WindowTitle     delimited by size
                " - "              delimited by size
                ls-temp            delimited by "  "
                x"00"              delimited by size
                into ls-DialogTitle
         End-string
         invoke os-Dialog "setTitleZ" using ls-DialogTitle

         set Field-Name                        to true
         move rt-namelength(ws-CurrentRectype) to Dialog-length
         invoke os-Dialog "setTheLength" using Dialog-Params


        End Method "initTitleAndLength".
        *>-----------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "messageBox".
        *>-----------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 ws-Windowtitle    pic x(18) value z"Description Codes".
        78 ML                         value 45.
        01 ws-MsgA.
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Blank or non-numeric key".              *>1
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Can't have a blank name".               *>2
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Invalid Component Code".                *>3
        05 pic x(ML) value
            z"Key must start 'F' 'G' 'I' 'L' or 'U'".                *>4
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Missing Other1 Level".                  *>5
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Missing Other2 Level".                  *>6
        05 pic x(ML) value z"OK to delete this record ?".            *>7
        05 pic x(ML) value z"Program Indexing error".                *>8
        01 ws-MsgB redefines ws-MsgA occurs 8 pic x(ML).

        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-MsgBox              object reference.
        01 ls-MessageText         pic x(ML).

        linkage section.
        01 lnk-response             pic x(4) comp-5.

        Procedure Division returning lnk-response.

         invoke MessageBox "new" using os-Dialog returning ls-MsgBox
         invoke ls-MsgBox "setTitleZ" using ws-Windowtitle
         move ws-MsgB(ValidationFlag) to ls-MessageText

         evaluate true
           when OktoDelete
              invoke ls-MsgBox "setTypeInformation"
              invoke ls-MsgBox "okCancel"
           when LogicError
              invoke ls-MsgBox "setTypeCritical"
              invoke ls-MsgBox "ok"
           when other
              invoke ls-MsgBox "setTypeWarning"
              invoke ls-MsgBox "ok"
         End-evaluate

         invoke ls-MsgBox "setMessageZ" using ls-MessageText
         invoke ls-MsgBox "show" returning lnk-response
         invoke ls-MsgBox "finalize" returning ls-MsgBox

        End Method "messageBox".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "passEntryfield".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-CodeX                          pic x(02).
        01 ls-length                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-text.
           05 occurs 1 to TextLength
              depending on ls-length     pic x(01).
        Procedure Division.

         evaluate true
           when Field-PrimeKey
                move length of DESCRIP-DesCode to Dialog-Length
                move DESCRIP-DesCode           to Dialog-text

           when field-name
                move length of DESCRIP-DesName to Dialog-Length
                move DESCRIP-DesName           to Dialog-text

           when field-OtherCode

                Evaluate true
                  when ws-CurrentRectype = ITEM-NAME-rectype
                       invoke os-ItemNames "getComponentAlphakey"
                              using DESCRIP-DesOther1 returning ls-CodeX
                       move length of ls-Codex to Dialog-Length
                       move ls-Codex           to Dialog-text

                  when ws-CurrentRectype = LENGTH-rectype
                       move length of DESCRIP-DesOther1 to Dialog-Length
                       move DESCRIP-DesOther1           to Dialog-text
                End-evaluate

           when field-Other1
                move length of DESCRIP-DesOther1 to Dialog-Length
                move DESCRIP-DesOther1           to Dialog-text

           when field-Other2
                move length of DESCRIP-DesOther2 to Dialog-Length
                move DESCRIP-DesOther2           to Dialog-text

         End-evaluate

         invoke os-Dialog "setEntryfield"
                using Dialog-Params, ls-length, ls-text

        End Method "passEntryfield".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "returnMenuchoice".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-choice                    pic x(4) comp-5.
        Procedure Division using lnk-choice.

        Evaluate lnk-choice
           when 998 invoke self "HelpFromMenu"
           when 999 invoke self "PB-Exit"

           when other
                invoke os-Menu "hide"
                move lnk-choice to ws-CurrentRecType
                set ByName       to true
                invoke self "createDescripsCollection"
        End-evaluate

        End Method "returnMenuchoice".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "rewriteRecord".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ls==.
        Procedure Division.

         invoke os-DesTable "rewriteRecord"
           using DESCRIp-record returning ws-SqlResult

         Evaluate true
            when ResultOK
              initialize ls-DesListRecord
              move DESCRIP-DesID     to Des-ID
              move DESCRIP-DesCode   to Des-Code
              move DESCRIP-DesName   to Des-Name
              move DESCRIP-DesOther1 to Des-Other1
              move DESCRIP-DesOther2 to Des-Other2

              invoke os-DescripsDBI "changeCollection"
              using     ws-CollectionParams,
                        ws-CurrentIndex,
                        ls-DesListRecord,
                        os-Collection
              returning os-Collection
              set Dialog-Object to os-Collection
              set field-Listbox to true
              invoke os-Dialog "setListboxContents"
                using  Dialog-Params
              invoke self "DisplayEmptyScreen"

            when TableError
               invoke self "PB-Exit"

         End-evaluate

        End Method "rewriteRecord".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "showMenu".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
            invoke os-Dialog "hide"
            invoke os-Menu   "show"
        End Method "showMenu".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "ValidationRoutine".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

         set ValidationOK     to true
         set ValidationReturn to true

         perform varying Dialog-Field from 2 by 1
                 until Dialog-Field > ws-LastField

            invoke os-Dialog "returnEntryField"
                   using Dialog-Field, Dialog-ReturnType

            if   ValidationError
                 invoke os-Dialog "setNextFocusEmpty" using Dialog-Params
                 EXIT METHOD
            End-if
         End-perform

        End Method "ValidationRoutine".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "writeRecord".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ls==.
        Procedure Division.

         invoke os-DesTable "writeRecord"
                using DESCRIp-record returning ws-SqlResult

         Evaluate true
            when ResultOK
              initialize ls-DesListRecord
              move DESCRIP-DesID     to Des-ID
              move DESCRIP-DesCode   to Des-Code
              move DESCRIP-DesName   to Des-Name
              move DESCRIP-DesOther1 to Des-Other1
              move DESCRIP-DesOther2 to Des-Other2

              invoke os-DescripsDBI "addToCollection"
                 using     ws-CollectionParams
                           ls-DesListRecord
                           os-Collection
                 returning os-Collection
              set Dialog-Object to os-Collection
              set field-Listbox to true
              invoke os-Dialog "setListboxContents"
                using  Dialog-Params
              invoke self "DisplayEmptyScreen"

             when TableError
                  invoke self "PB-Exit"
         End-evaluate

        End Method "writeRecord".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------

        *> ++++ Return entries from Dialog :-

        *>       CB(Checkbox)
        *>       EF(Entryfield)
        *>       DL(DropList)
        *>       LB(Listbox)
        *>       PB(Pushbutton)
        *>       RB(RadioButton)
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------

        *> Key                  y
        *> Name                      y
        *> OtherCode                     y
        *> Other1                            y
        *> Other2                                y
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        *> All types             x   x   -   -   -
        *> Length(** 1)          x   x   x   -   -
        *> Name  (** 2)          x   x   x   -   -
        *> Points(** 3)          x   x   x   -   -
        *> Techs                 x   x   -   x   x
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        *> ** 1 - Check code(1:1) for Validity; display OtherCode
        *> ** 2 - Check Component Code and display Other Code
        *> ** 3 - Check code(1:1) = "X" & display OtherCode "Exception"
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-name".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\dlgReturn.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        *>----------------dilgreturn.cpy ------------------------------

        01  lnk-ReturnValues.

           *> Column and Line used to identify the 'cell' from a
           *> two-dimensional table

           05 lnk-Column                  pic x(4) comp-5.
           05 lnk-Line                    pic x(4) comp-5.
           05 lnk-length                  pic x(4) comp-5.

           *> Field-ID used where necessary to return a specific
           *> selection, such as the choice from a Radio Button Group

           05 lnk-FieldID                 pic x(4) comp-5.

           05 lnk-text.
              10 occurs 1 to ws-MaxLength
                 depending on lnk-length  pic x(01).

        *>--------------------------------------------------------------

        Procedure Division using lnk-ReturnValues.

        set RecordChanged to true

        if    lnk-text = spaces
              set ErrorName to true
              invoke self "messageBox"
              invoke os-Dialog "setnextfocusEmpty" using Dialog-Params
              EXIT METHOD

        else  move lnk-text to DESCRIP-DesName
        End-if

        if   ws-CurrentRectype = POINT-rectype
             perform CHECK-POINTS
        End-if

        EXIT METHOD.

        CHECK-POINTS.

        if   DESCRIP-DesCode(1:1) = "X"
             move "Exception" to DESCRIP-DesOther1

        else move spaces to DESCRIP-DesOther1
        End-if

        .
        End Method "EF-name".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-othercode".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\dlgReturn.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using lnk-ReturnValues.

         set RecordChanged to true

         if   ws-CurrentRectype = ITEM-NAME-rectype
             invoke self "checkItemComponent" using lnk-text
         End-if

        End Method "EF-othercode".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-Other1".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\dlgReturn.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using lnk-ReturnValues.

           set RecordChanged to true
           move lnk-text to DESCRIP-DesOther1
           invoke os-Dialog "setFocusDefault"

        End Method "EF-Other1".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-Other2".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\dlgReturn.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using lnk-ReturnValues.

           set RecordChanged to true
           move lnk-text to DESCRIP-DesOther2

           if   RecordNotFound
                set field-Other2 to true
                invoke os-Dialog "setNextFocusEmpty" using Dialog-Params

           else invoke os-Dialog "setFocusDefault"
           End-if

        End Method "EF-Other2".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-primekey".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-result                    pic 9(03).
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\dlgReturn.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using lnk-ReturnValues.

          Evaluate true
            when  lnk-text = spaces
                  invoke self "DisplayEmptyScreen"
                  EXIT METHOD

            when  ws-CurrentRectype = LENGTH-rectype
                  invoke self "EF-Primekey2"
                         using lnk-length lnk-text
                         returning ls-result

                  if ls-result <> zeroes
                     set Field-PrimeKey to true
                     invoke os-Dialog "setNextFocusEmpty"
                            using Dialog-Params
                     EXIT METHOD
                  End-if

          End-evaluate

          move lnk-text to ws-key
          invoke self "checkRecordExists" using ws-PrimeKey

        End Method "EF-primekey".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "EF-Primekey2".
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        78 TableSize                    value 5.
        78 TL                           value 12.
        01 wt1.
           05 pic x(TL) value "F,Feet".
           05 pic x(TL) value "G,Gallon-Imp".
           05 pic x(TL) value "I,inches".
           05 pic x(TL) value "L,Litres".
           05 pic x(TL) value "U,US-Gallon".
        01 wt2 redefines wt1.
           05 wt3 occurs TableSize.
              10 ws-char                pic x.
              10                        pic x.
              10 ws-code                pic x(10).

        Local-storage section.
        01 n                            pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-text                      pic x(04).

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-length                   pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 lnk-text.
           05 occurs 1 to TextLength
              depending on lnk-length   pic x(01).
        01 lnk-result                   pic 9(03).

        Procedure Division using     lnk-length lnk-text
                           returning lnk-result.


          move function upper-case (lnk-text) to ls-text
          move 99 to lnk-result
          perform varying n from 1 by 1 until n > TableSize

             if ls-text(1:1)     = ws-char(n)
                move zeroes       to lnk-result
                move ls-text      to ws-key
                move ws-code(n)   to ws-suffix
                Exit perform
             End-if
          End-perform

          if    lnk-result <> zeroes
                set ErrorLengthKey to true
                invoke self "messageBox"
          End-if

        End Method "EF-Primekey2".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "LB-index".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Index                     pic x(4) comp-5.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Index.

          move lnk-Index to ws-CurrentIndex
          invoke os-DescripsDBI "getKeyFromIndex"
             using ws-CurrentIndex returning ws-Key

          if   ws-Key <> spaces
               invoke self "checkRecordExists" using ws-PrimeKey
          End-if

        End Method "LB-index".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-cancel".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.
          invoke self "DisplayEmptyScreen"
        End Method "PB-cancel".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-delete".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-response                            pic x(4) comp-5.

        Procedure Division.

         if  RecordFound
             set OKtoDelete to true
             invoke self "messageBox" returning ls-response

             if ls-response = mb-return-ok
                invoke os-DesTable "deleteRecord"
                       using     DESCRIP-DesID
                                 DESCRIP-DesCode
                       returning ws-SqlResult

                if  ResultOK
                    invoke os-DescripsDBI "deleteFromCollection"
                           using     ws-CurrentIndex
                                     os-Collection
                           returning os-Collection
                    set Dialog-Object to os-Collection
                    set field-Listbox to true
                    invoke os-Dialog "setListboxContents"
                      using  Dialog-Params
                End-if

              End-if
         End-if

         if ContinueProgram
            invoke self "DisplayEmptyScreen"
         End-if

        End Method "PB-delete".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-Exit".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.
         set CancelProgram to true
         invoke os-Dialog "hide"
         invoke os-Menu "hide"
         invoke self "finalizeObjects"
        End Method "PB-Exit".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-help".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
         invoke CtHelp "helpFile" using os-Parent
         invoke self "showMenu"
        End Method "PB-help".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-nextMenuChoice".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.
         invoke self "showMenu"
        End Method "PB-nextMenuChoice".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-ok".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 n                                pic x(4) comp-5.
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Flag                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        Procedure Division using lnk-Flag.

        *> If individual entries have been returned before user clicks
        *> PB-OK, then "RecordChanged" will have alredy been set

        if     RecordNotChanged
               move lnk-Flag to RecordChangedFlag
        End-if

        if     RecordChanged
               perform VALIDATE-RECORD

        else   invoke self "displayEmptyScreen"
        End-if

        EXIT METHOD.

        VALIDATE-RECORD.

         set ValidationOK to true
         invoke self "validationRoutine"

         If ValidationOK

             if     RecordFound
                    invoke self "rewriteRecord"

             else   invoke self "writeRecord"
             End-if

             invoke self "displayEmptyScreen"

         End-if
         .
        End Method "PB-ok".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-sequenceByKey".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.

          if not ByKey
             set ByKey to true
             invoke self "createDescripsCollection"
          End-if

        End Method "PB-sequenceByKey".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-sequenceByName".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.

          if not ByName
             set ByName to true
             invoke self "createDescripsCollection"
          End-if
        End Method "PB-sequenceByName".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "PB-sequenceByOther".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Procedure Division.

          if not ByOther
             Evaluate true
               when ws-CurrentRectype = ITEM-NAME-rectype
               when ws-CurrentRectype = LENGTH-rectype
               when ws-CurrentRectype = POINT-rectype
               when ws-CurrentRectype = TECHNICIAN-NAME-rectype
                    set ByOther to true
                    invoke self "createDescripsCollection"
              End-evaluate
          End-if

        End Method "PB-sequenceByOther".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------

        End OBJECT.
        End CLASS DescripsEdit.

       *>---------------------------------------------------------------

*** DBI MAIN contains all common routines required by sub-classes 
prefixed "DBI"

Rather than copy/paste or try to remember collection creation syntax, it 
is all included in this class - in fact this is the only class in which 
I include direct references to the Collection support classes. The 
remainder of the program is used for creating/changing/searching 
collections.
        *>-----------------------dbimain.cbl ---------------------------

        copy "\copylib\dbimain.cbl".
        *>-----------------------dbimain.cbl ---------------------------

        Class-id.          DbiMain
                           inherits from Base.

        Class-control.     DbiMain                 is class "dbimain"

                           Array                   is class "array"
                           Association             is class "associtn"
                           Callback                is class "callback"
                           CharacterArray          is class "chararry"
                           Cobolcomp5              is class "comp5"
                           Cobolpicx               is class "picx"
                           Dictionary              is class "dictinry"
                           OrderedCollection       is class "ordrdcll"
                           SortedCollection        is class "srtdclln"
                           .

        *> Errors displayed are not in Windows GUI format because these
        *> errors occur as a result of coding and development testing -
        *> so they are DOS Text display with a STOP RUN.

        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        FACTORY.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        END FACTORY.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        OBJECT.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        OBJECT-STORAGE SECTION.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy"  replacing ==(tag)== by ==ws==.
        copy "\copylib\lnkObjVal.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ws==.

        01 n                                       pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 charx                                   pic x.
        01 ws-Kounter                              pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ws-KounterDisplay                       pic zzzzz9.
        01 ErrorFlag                               pic x(4) comp-5.
           88 Error-Type                           value 1.
           88 Error-Sequence                       value 2.
           88 Error-RefOrValues                    value 3.
           88 Error-RecordLength                   value 4.
           88 Error-DictionaryLength               value 5.
           88 Error-DictionaryKey                  value 6.
           88 Error-ObjectFromKey                  value 7.
           88 Error-ChangeNoIndex                  value 8.
           88 Error-UnequalObjects                 value 9.

        01 ws-Key.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-KeyLength            pic x.

        01 ws-Pos.
           10 PosName       pic 9(03).
           10 PosKey        pic 9(03).
           10 PosOther      pic 9(03).

        01 os-List                  object reference value null.
        01 os-OldString             object reference value null.

        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "addToCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-string                             object reference.
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-record.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-RecordLength            pic x.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Record.

         Evaluate true
           when ofReferences
                invoke CharacterArray "withLengthValue" using
                   ws-RecordLength, lnk-record returning ls-string
                invoke os-List "add"
                         using ls-string returning ls-string
           when other
                invoke os-List "add" using lnk-record
         End-Evaluate

        End Method "addToCollection".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "addToDictionary".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Key.
           05 occurs 1 to 100 depending
              on ws-KeyLength                   pic x.
        01 lnk-Data.
           05 occurs 1 to 100 depending
              on ws-DataLength                  pic x.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Key, lnk-Data.

         invoke os-List "atput"
                using lnk-key, lnk-data

        End Method "addToDictionary".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "changeCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-Index1                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-Index2                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-string1                        object reference.
        01 ls-string2                        object reference.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-index                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 lnk-record.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-RecordLength           pic x.

        Procedure division using lnk-Index, lnk-Record.

        invoke CharacterArray "withLengthValue" using
               ws-RecordLength, lnk-record returning ls-string2
        move lnk-index to ls-Index1 ls-Index2
        invoke os-List "at"
               using ls-index1 returning ls-string1
        invoke os-List "replaceAll"
               using ls-string1 ls-string2 ls-index1 ls-index2

        End Method "changeCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "changeWithNoIndex".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        *> As a result of changing a Droplist inter-acting with a
        *> Dialog used in conjunction with say, a Treeview, the
        *> 'parent' class will not have an :-

        *> 'invoke ls-Object "selectedItem" returning ls-index'

        *> Where no Index is supplied objects are compared
        *> in "CheckObjects" to establish the index of the
        *> Element to be changed

        *> Local-storage section.
        01 ls-NewString                         object reference.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Strings.
           05 lnk-OldString                      object reference.
           05 lnk-NewString                      object reference.

        Procedure division using lnk-Strings.

        set os-OldString     to lnk-OldString
        initialize              ws-ObjectValues
        move ws-RecordLength to ws-RecLength
        set ws-ObjectString  to null
        invoke self "compareObjects"

        if   ws-Index <> zeroes
             invoke os-List "replaceAll"
                  using os-OldString, lnk-NewString, ws-index ws-index

        else set Error-ChangeNoIndex to true
             invoke self "showError"
        End-if

        End Method "changeWithNoIndex".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "CheckObjects".          *> Callback   PRIVATE
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

        *> Using method "KeysAndDataDo", the index and element are
        *> automaticaly passed to this method

        01 ls-Bool                      pic 99 comp-5.
           88 IsTrue                    value 1.
           88 isFalse                   value 0.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Index                    pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 lnk-Element                  object reference.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Index, lnk-Element.

        *> Having read the N/E V 4.0 OO Book, could have coded this as
        *>
        *> if os-Oldstring = lnk-Element
        *>    set isTrue to true.........

           invoke os-OldString "equal"
                  using lnk-Element returning ls-Bool

           if IsTrue
              move lnk-Index to ws-Index
              invoke os-List "quitIteration"
           End-if

        Exit Method.
        End Method "CheckObjects".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "checkParameters".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *>  1 - Collection Types :
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *>  TypeOrdered  :
        *>  TypeSorted   :
        *>  TypeDroplist :

        *>  -  ofReferences   y  y  y  y  n  n  n  n
        *>  -  ofValues       y  y  n  n  y  y  n  n
        *> RecordLength ?     y  n  y  n  y  n  y  n
        *>---------------------------------------------------------
        *> Actions
        *>---------------------------------------------------------
        *> N/A                x  x  x  x  x  -  x  -
        *> Error              -  -  -  -  -  x  -  x
        *>----------------------------------------------------------

        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *> 2 - Dictionary Types :
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *>  TypeDictionary :
        *>  - Data/NameLength   y  y  n  n
        *>  - KeyLength         y  n  y  n
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *> Actions :
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        *> N/A                  x  -  -  -
        *> Error                -  x  x  x
        *>----------------------------------------------------------

        if not ValidType
               set Error-Type to true
               invoke self "showError"
               EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        if not ValidSequence
               set Error-Sequence to true
               invoke self "showError"
               EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        if     ws-size = zeroes
               move 10 to ws-size
        End-if

        if not TypeDictionary
               perform COLLECTION-CHECKS

        else   perfoRM DICTIONARY-CHECKS
        end-if

        EXIT METHOD.

        COLLECTION-CHECKS.

        if not ValidRefValues
             set Error-RefOrValues to true
             invoke self "showError"
             EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        if   ws-RecordLength = zeroes
             set Error-RecordLength to true
             invoke self "showError"
             EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        .
        DICTIONARY-CHECKS.

        if   ws-NameLength = zeroes
             set Error-DictionaryLength to true
             invoke self "showError"
             EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        if   ws-KeyLength = zeroes
             set Error-DictionaryKey to true
             invoke self "showError"
             EXIT METHOD
        End-if

        .

        End Method "checkParameters".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "compareObjects".    *> create Callback PRIVATE
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        01 ls-Callback                      object reference.

        move zeroes  to ws-Index
        invoke Callback "new" using     self "CheckObjects "
                              returning ls-Callback
        invoke os-List "KeysAndDataDo" using ls-Callback
        invoke ls-Callback "finalize" returning ls-Callback

        *> Note :  when using Method "KeysandDataDo", for each
        *>         iteration the invoke passes (1) Index and (2) Element

        End Method "compareObjects".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "deleteFromCollection".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        01 ls-string                         object reference.
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-index                         pic x(4) comp-5.

        Procedure Division using lnk-index.

          invoke os-List "removeAtIndex"
                 using lnk-index returning ls-string

        End Method "deleteFromCollection".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "deleteWithNoIndex".    *> Creates a Callback
        *>------------------------------------------------------------

        *> As a result of changing a Droplist inter-acting with a
        *> Dialog used in conjunction with say, a Treeview, the
        *> 'parent' class will not have an :-

        *> 'invoke ls-Object "selectedItem" returning ls-index'

        *> Where no Index is supplied objects are compared in
        *> "CheckObjects" to establish the index of the
        *> Element to be deleted

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-record.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-RecordLength           pic x.

        Procedure division using lnk-Record.

        invoke CharacterArray "withLengthValue" using
               ws-RecordLength, lnk-record returning os-OldString

        invoke self "compareObjects"

        if  ws-Index <> zeroes
            invoke os-List "removeAtIndex"
               using ws-index returning os-OldString
        End-if

        End Method "deleteWithNoIndex".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "DisplayList". *> Test - invoked from requesting class
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        01 ls-Callback                      object reference.

        move zeroes to n, ws-Kounter
        Evaluate true
          when TypeDictionary
             invoke Callback "new"
             using self "DisplayDictionaryVal "
             returning ls-Callback
             invoke os-List "KeysAndDataDo" using ls-Callback

          when other

             Evaluate true
               when ofReferences
                  invoke Callback "new"
                    using self "DisplayCollectionRef "
                    returning ls-Callback
               when other
                  invoke Callback "new"
                  using self "DisplayCollectionVal "
                  returning ls-Callback
              End-Evaluate

              invoke os-List "do" using ls-Callback

        End-Evaluate

        move ws-Kounter to ws-KounterDisplay
        display "Elements displayed =    ", ws-KounterDisplay
        accept charx
        invoke ls-Callback "finalize" returning ls-Callback

        End Method "DisplayList".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "displayCollectionRef".        *> PRIVATE
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        01 ls-Length                            pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-Text                              pic x(100).
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Element                          object reference.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Element.

         invoke lnk-Element "sizeInBytes" returning ls-Length
         invoke lnk-Element "getValueWithSize"
                   using ls-Length returning ls-Text
         invoke self "displayCollection2" using ls-text

        End Method "displayCollectionRef".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "displayCollectionVal".           *> PRIVATE
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Element              object reference.
        01 lnk-Text.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-RecordLength           pic x.

        Procedure division using lnk-Element.
         invoke self "displayCollection2" using lnk-Element

        End Method "displayCollectionVal".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "DisplayCollection2".           *> PRIVATE
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 Line1 pic x(80) value
        ".........1.........2.........3.........4.........5.........6....
       -".....7.........8".

        01 Line2 pic x(80) value
        ".........0.........0.........0.........0.........0.........0....
       -".....0.........0".

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Text.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-RecordLength           pic x.

        Procedure division using lnk-Text.

         inspect lnk-Text replacing all x"09" by "^"
         inspect lnk-Text replacing all x"00" by "~"

         if n = 0
            perform HEADER-LINES

         else add 1 to n
         End-if

         if   n > 23
              accept charx
              perform HEADER-LINES

         else add 1 to ws-Kounter
              move ws-Kounter to ws-KounterDisplay
              display ws-KounterDisplay " " lnk-text(1:ws-RecordLength)
         End-if

        EXIT METHOD
        .

        HEADER-LINES.

        display Line1
        display Line2
        move 3 to n
        .
        End Method "DisplayCollection2".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "displayDictionaryVal".           *> PRIVATE
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 Line1 pic x(80) value
        ".........1.........2.........3.........4.........5.........6....
       -".....7.........8".

        01 Line2 pic x(80) value
        ".........0.........0.........0.........0.........0.........0....
       -".....0.........0".

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Record.
              10 occurs 1 to 100
                 depending on ws-RecordLength              pic x.

        Procedure division using lnk-Record.

         inspect lnk-Record replacing all x"09" by "^"

         if n = 0
            perform HEADER-LINES

         else add 1 to n
         End-if

         if   n > 23
              accept charx
              perform HEADER-LINES

         else add 1 to ws-Kounter
              move ws-Kounter to ws-KounterDisplay
              display
               ws-KounterDisplay " " lnk-record(1:ws-RecordLength)
         End-if

        EXIT METHOD
        .

        HEADER-LINES.

        display Line1
        display Line2
        move 3 to n
        .
        End Method "displayDictionaryVal".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "finalizeObjects".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Local-storage section.
        copy "\copylib\sqlresult.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==01 ls==.
        01 ls-object                         object reference.

           *> NOT currently used

        End Method "finalizeObjects".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getObjectFromIndex".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-index-In                      pic x(4) comp-5.
        copy "\copylib\lnkObjVal.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-Index-In
                           returning lnk-ObjectValues.

        move lnk-Index-In     to ws-Index
        set  ws-ObjectString  to null
        move ws-RecordLength  to ws-RecLength
        initialize               ws-Record


        invoke os-List "at"
               using ws-index returning ws-ObjectString
        invoke ws-ObjectString "getValuewithSize"
               using ws-RecLength returning ws-record
        move ws-ObjectValues to lnk-ObjectValues

        Exit Method.
        End Method "getObjectFromIndex".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getObjectFromKey".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        01 ls-Callback                  object reference.
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Key.
           05 occurs 1 to 100
              depending on ws-KeyLength           pic x.
        copy "\copylib\lnkObjVal.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-Key
                           returning lnk-ObjectValues.

        *> TEST----------
        *>invoke self "displayList"

        move lnk-key          to ws-Key
        move zeroes           to ws-Index
        set ws-ObjectString   to null
        move ws-RecordLength  to ws-RecLength
        initialize               ws-Record

        invoke Callback "new"  using     self "getObjectFromKey2 "
                               returning ls-Callback
        invoke os-List "KeysAndDataDo" using ls-Callback
        move ws-ObjectValues to lnk-ObjectValues
        set lnk-objectString to ws-ObjectString

        if  lnk-Index = zeroes OR
            lnk-ObjectString = null
            set Error-ObjectFromKey to true
            invoke self "showError"
        End-if

        invoke ls-Callback "finalize" returning ls-Callback

        End Method "getObjectFromKey".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getObjectFromKey2".        *> Callback  PRIVATE
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        *> Using method "KeysAndDataDo", the index and element are
        *> automaticaly passed to this method

         01 ls-Length                   pic x(4) comp-5.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Index                    pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 lnk-Element                  object reference.

        Procedure Division using lnk-Index, lnk-Element.

        invoke lnk-Element "sizeInBytes" returning ls-Length
        invoke lnk-Element "getValueWithSize"
                  using ls-Length returning ws-Record

        *> ws-Key is in Working-Storage

        if ws-Key(1:ws-KeyLength) =
           ws-Record(PosKey:ws-KeyLength)
           move lnk-Index       to ws-Index
           set  ws-ObjectString to lnk-Element
           invoke os-List "quitIteration"
        End-if

        End Method "getObjectFromKey2".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "initDictionary".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        01 ls-AssocTemplate         object reference value null.
        01 ls-DataTemplate          object reference value null.
        01 ls-KeyTemplate           object reference value null.

        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-Dictionary                    object reference.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                           returning lnk-Dictionary.

        move lnk-CollectionParams to ws-CollectionParams
        invoke self "checkParameters"

        invoke CobolPicx   "newclass"   using     ws-KeyLength
                                        returning ls-KeyTemplate
        invoke CobolPicx   "newclass"   using     ws-DataLength
                                        returning ls-DataTemplate
        invoke Association "newclass"   using     ls-KeyTemplate
                                                  ls-DataTemplate
                                        returning ls-AssocTemplate

        Evaluate true
          when ofValues
               invoke Dictionary "ofValues"
                      using     ls-AssocTemplate
                                ws-DataLength
                      returning os-List
               set lnk-Dictionary to os-List

        End-evaluate

        invoke ls-AssocTemplate "finalize" returning ls-AssocTemplate
        invoke ls-DataTemplate  "finalize" returning ls-DataTemplate
        invoke ls-KeyTemplate   "finalize" returning ls-KeyTemplate

        End Method "initDictionary".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "initOrderedCollection".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        *> Local-storage section.
        01 ls-Template                      object reference.
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-Pos.
           05 occurs 3 pic 9(03).

        01 lnk-Collection                     object reference.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                                     lnk-Pos
                           returning lnk-Collection.

        move lnk-CollectionParams to ws-CollectionParams
        move lnk-Pos              to ws-Pos
        invoke self "checkParameters"

        Evaluate true
          when ofReferences
               invoke OrderedCollection "ofReferences"
                      using     ws-size
                      returning os-List
               set lnk-Collection to os-List

          when ofValues
               invoke CobolPicx "newClass" using ws-RecordLength
                      returning ls-template
               invoke OrderedCollection "ofValues"
                      using     ls-template, ws-size
                      returning os-List
               set lnk-Collection to os-List
        End-evaluate

        End Method "initOrderedCollection".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "initSortedCollection".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        *> Local-storage section.
        01 ls-Template                      object reference.
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-Pos.
           05 occurs 3 pic 9(03).

        01 lnk-Collection                     object reference.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                                     lnk-Pos
                           returning lnk-Collection.

        move lnk-CollectionParams to ws-CollectionParams
        move lnk-Pos              to ws-Pos
        invoke self "checkParameters"

        Evaluate true
          when ofReferences
               invoke SortedCollection "ofReferences"
                      using     ws-size
                      returning os-List
               set lnk-Collection to os-List

          when ofValues
               invoke CobolPicx "newClass" using ws-RecordLength
                      returning ls-template
               invoke SortedCollection "ofValues"
                      using     ls-template, ws-size
                      returning os-List
               set lnk-Collection to os-List
        End-evaluate

        End Method "initSortedCollection".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "setOslist".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        *> When using "CopyEmptyWithSize" in the invoker, the new
        *> reference to the revised list is passed to this 'super'.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-List                     object reference.
        Procedure Division using lnk-List.
        set os-List to lnk-List
        End Method "setOslist".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "showError".               *> PRIVATE
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        78 ML                            value 50.
        78 MN                            value 9.
        01 T1.
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - Type".                     *> 1
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - Sequence".                 *> 2
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - RefOrValues".              *> 3
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - RecordLength".             *> 4
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - DictionaryLength".         *> 5
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - DictionaryKey".            *> 6
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - ObjectFromKey".            *> 7
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - ChangeNoIndex".            *> 8
         05 pic x(ML) value "Error - Non-matching objects".     *> 9

        01 T2 redefines T1.
         05 T3 occurs MN pic x(ML).

           display T3(ErrorFlag)
           accept charx
           STOP RUN

        End Method "showError".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------

        END OBJECT.
        End CLASS DbiMain.



*>----------------------------------------------------------------------
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------


*** DBI DESCRIPTONS - INHERITS FROM DBI MAIN ABOVE :

*>---------------------------- dbides.cbl -----------------------------

        Class-id.          DescripsDBI
                           inherits from DbiMain.

        Class-control.     DbiMain                 is class "dbimain"
                           DescripsDBI             is class "dbides"

                           Array                   is class "array"
                           CharacterArray          is class "chararry"
                           Cobolcomp5              is class "comp5"
                           .

        *> NOTE : For changes to DESCRIP-records, (held in the DB),
        *> copyfile "tabdes.cpy" is used. For changes to Collections/
        *> Dictionaries, copyfile "deslist.cpy" is used
        *>
        *> While Schedule Nos. are not part of the DesTable - routines to
        *> access them are included here for convenience because they are
        *> part of the 'descriptive set'

        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        FACTORY.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        End FACTORY.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        OBJECT.
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        OBJECT-STORAGE SECTION.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy"   replacing ==(tag)== by ==ws==.
*>--------------------- collection.cpy-------------------------------

        *> Note : the pic x(4) comp-5's are required by M/F classes

        01  ws-CollectionParams.

            10 ws-DataLength               pic x(4) comp-5.
            10 ws-NameLength
               redefines ws-DataLength     pic x(4) comp-5.
            10 ws-KeyLength                pic x(4) comp-5.
            10 ws-RecordLength             pic x(4) comp-5.

            10 ws-RefOrValues              pic 9.
               88 ofReferences                value 1.
               88 ofValues                    value 2.
               88 ValidRefValues              value 1 thru 2.

            10 ws-sequence                 pic 9(02).
               88 ByName                      value 1.
               88 ByKey                       value 2.
               88 ByOther                     value 3.
               88 ByItem                      value 4.
               88 ByKeyOnly                   value 5.
               88 ByKeyAndName                value 6.
               88 ByKeyAndData                value 7.
               88 ByKeyAndOther               value 8.
               88 ByNameAndKey                value 9.

               88 RmPointsDictionary          value 20.

               88 ValidSequence               value 1 thru 9, 20.

            10 ws-size                     pic x(4) comp-5.

            10 ws-type                     pic 9(02).
               88 TypeDictionary              value 1.
               88 TypeDropList                value 2.
               88 TypeOrdered                 value 3.
               88 TypeSorted                  value 4.
               88 TypeDummyDropList           value 5.
               88 ValidType                   value 1 thru 5.
               88 TypeTabbed                  value 3 thru 4. *> x"09"

*>-------------------------------------------------------------------

        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ws==.
        *>---------------- deslist.cpy ---------------------------------

        01  ws-DesListRecord.
           05 Des-ID                    pic 9(02).
           05 Des-Code                  pic x(04).
           05 Tab1                      pic x.
           05 Des-Name                  pic x(40).
           05 Tab2                      pic x.
           05 Des-Other1                pic x(10).
           05 Des-Other2                pic x(10).

        *>---------------------------------------------------------------

        01 charx                           pic x.

        01 DisplayFlag                     pic 9 value 0.
           88 DisplayList                  value 1.
           88 DontDisplayList              value 0.

        *> Listbox records :-

        *> ByName (Name, Key, Other)
        *>0                                        4    4
        *>1                                        2    7
 
*>nnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnn^kkkk^OOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO

        01 ByNameA.
           05 PosName    pic 9(03) value 01.
           05 PosKey     pic 9(03) value 42.
           05 PosOther   pic 9(03) value 47.

        01 Name-Record.
           05 Des-Name                     pic x(40).
           05 Tab1                         pic x.
           05 Des-Code                     pic x(04).
           05 Tab2                         pic x.
           05 Des-Other1                   pic x(10).
           05 Des-Other2                   pic x(10).

        *> ByKey (Key, Name, Other)
        *>0    0                                        4
        *>1    6                                        7
        *>kkkk^nnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnn^OOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO

        01 ByKeyA.
           05 PosKey     pic 9(03) value 01.
           05 PosName    pic 9(03) value 06.
           05 PosOther   pic 9(03) value 47.

        01 Key-Record.
           05 Des-Code                     pic x(04).
           05 Tab1                         pic x.
           05 Des-Name                     pic x(40).
           05 Tab2                         pic x.
           05 Des-Other1                   pic x(10).
           05 Des-Other2                   pic x(10).


        *> ByOther (Other, Name, Key)
        *>0                    2                                        4
        *>1                    2                                        4
        *>ooooooooooOOOOOOOOOO^nnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnnn^k
        *>

        01 ByOtherA.
           05 PosOther   pic 9(03) value 01.
           05 PosName    pic 9(03) value 22.
           05 PosKey     pic 9(03) value 44.

        01 Other-Record.
           05 Des-Other1                   pic x(10).
           05 Des-Other2                   pic x(10).
           05 Tab1                         pic x.
           05 Des-Name                     pic x(40).
           05 Tab2                         pic x.
           05 Des-Code                     pic x(04).

        01 ws-Pos.
           05 PosName           pic 9(03).
           05 PosKey            pic 9(03).
           05 PosOther          pic 9(03).

        01 ws-TempRecord                   pic x(66).
        01 ws-LastNumber                   pic 9(03).

        *> OBJECTS
        01 os-DesTable            object reference value null.
        01 os-List                object reference value null.

        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "begin".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Table                         object reference.
        Procedure Division using lnk-Table.
          set os-DesTable to lnk-Table
        End Method "begin".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "addToCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        *> also invoked from DesTable by iteration

        Linkage section.
        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using lnk-DesListRecord.
         move lnk-DesListRecord to ws-DesListRecord
         invoke self "makeListRecord"
         invoke super "addToCollection" using ws-TempRecord
        End Method "addToCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "changeCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-index                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-index
                                     lnk-DesListRecord.

          move lnk-DesListRecord to ws-DesListRecord
          invoke self "makeListRecord"
          invoke super "changeCollection"
                 using lnk-Index, ws-TempRecord

        End Method "changeCollection".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "createCollection".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 ws-MethodName pic x(30) value "AddToCollection".

        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)==  by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-Rectype                       pic 9(02).
        01 lnk-values.
         copy "\copylib\sqlResult.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==05 lnk==.
        *>----------sqlresult.cpy-------------------------------------

            05 lnk-SqlResult                        pic 9(03).

            88  ResultOK                    value 0.
            88  FileResultOK                value 0.

            88  RecNotFound                 value 1.

            88  NoMoreRows                  value 2.
            88  FileFinis                   value 2.

            88  DuplicateKey                value 3.

            88  DataError                   value 97.
            88  CursorError                 value 98.

            88  FileError                   value 99.
            88  TableError                  value 97 thru 99.

        *> This copyfile is multi-purpose with Level 88s used for either
        *> COBOL files or (R)DBMS Tables using SQLERROR or SQLSTATE

        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

         05 lnk-collection                 object reference.

        Procedure division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                                     lnk-Rectype
                           returning lnk-values.

         set ResultOK              to true
         set lnk-Collection        to null
         move zeroes               to ws-LastNumber
         move lnk-CollectionParams to ws-CollectionParams

         Evaluate true
           when ByName  move CORR ByNameA  to ws-Pos
           when ByKey   move CORR ByKeyA   to ws-Pos
           when ByOther move CORR ByOtherA to ws-Pos
         End-Evaluate

         invoke super "initSortedCollection"
                using       ws-CollectionParams
                            ws-Pos
                returning   os-List
         set lnk-Collection to os-List
         invoke os-DesTable "makeCollection"
                using       self
                            ws-MethodName
                            lnk-Rectype
                returning   lnk-SqlResult

         *>   NOTE : DesTable using iteration, invokes
         *>  "AddToCollection" in this Class

         if DisplayList
            invoke super "displayList"
         End-if


        End Method "createCollection".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "createDialogTabstops".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------
        *> NOTE : To use Tabs in a Listbox you need to set the property
        *> "Use Tabstops" for the Listbox control in the Dialog Editor.
        *> You have to do a bit of 'fiddling' with "78 Kounter" below
        *> using a value which gives you an aesthetically pleasing
        *> Listbox

        *> Rather than 'manually' figuring out the tab positioning, let
        *> the method calculate the positioning !

        01 n                        pic x(4) comp-5.
        78 tabcount                 value 2.
        78 Kounter                  value 10.
        01 TabsPos occurs tabcount  pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 TabsVal occurs tabcount  pic x(4) comp-5.

        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-tabstops             object reference.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                           returning lnk-tabstops.

          evaluate true
           when ByName
              compute TabsPos(1) =
                ( function length (Des-Name of Name-record ) + 1 )
              compute TabsPos(2) = TabsPos(1) +
                ( function length (Des-Code of Name-record ) + 1 )

           when ByKey
              compute TabsPos(1) =
                ( function length (Des-Code of Key-record ) + 1 )
              compute TabsPos(2) = TabsPos(1) +
                ( function length (Des-Name of Key-record ) + 1 )

           when ByOther
              compute TabsPos(1) =
                ( function length (Des-Other1 of Other-Record )) +
                ( function length (Des-Other2  of Other-Record )) +  1
              compute TabsPos(2) = TabsPos(1) +
                ( function length (Des-Name of Other-record )  + 1 )

          End-evaluate

          move tabcount to n
          invoke Array "ofValues" using     cobolcomp5, n
                                  returning lnk-tabstops

          perform varying n from 1 by 1 until n > tabcount
             multiply TabsPos(n) by Kounter giving TabsVal(n)
             invoke lnk-tabstops "atPut" using n TabsVal(n)
          End-perform

        End method "createDialogTabstops".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "createDictionary".
        *>--------------------------------------------------------------
        Working-storage section.
        01 ws-MethodName        pic x(30) value "newDictionaryRecord".
        Linkage section.
        copy "\copylib\collection.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.
        01 lnk-Rectype                       pic 9(02).
        01 lnk-values.
         copy "\copylib\sqlResult.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==05 lnk==.
         05 lnk-Dictionary                 object reference.

        Procedure division using     lnk-CollectionParams
                                     lnk-Rectype
                           returning lnk-values.

         set ResultOK              to true
         move zeroes               to ws-LastNumber
         move lnk-CollectionParams to ws-CollectionParams
         invoke super "initDictionary"
                using ws-CollectionParams returning os-List
         set lnk-Dictionary to os-List
         invoke super "makeCollection"
                using     self
                          ws-MethodName
                          lnk-RecType
                returning lnk-SqlResult

         *>   NOTE : super (DesTable) using iteration, invokes
         *>  "newDictionaryRecord" in this Class

        End Method "createDictionary".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "createScheduleCollection".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------

        *> As the following is a static list, the data is stored here for
        *> convenience, rather than create a file or DB table.

        Working-Storage section.
        01 s1 pic x(52) value
        "Std,XS ,XXS,10 ,20 ,30 ,40 ,60 ,80 ,100,120,140,160,".
        01 s2 redefines s1.
          05  occurs 13.
              10 ScheduleCode pic x(03).
              10              pic x.

        01 n                        pic 9(04).
        01 ls-length                pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-size                  pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-string                object reference.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Collection            object reference.

        Procedure division returning lnk-Collection.

         initialize                    ws-CollectionParams
         move length of Name-record to ws-NameLength
         move 13                    to ws-size
         set ofReferences           to true
         invoke super "initSortedCollection"
            using ws-CollectionParams returning os-List
         set lnk-Collection to os-List
         initialize Name-record

          perform varying n from 1 by 1 until n > 13

             move ScheduleCode(n) to Des-Name of Name-record
             move n               to Des-Code of Name-record

             if   OfReferences
                  move x"09" to Tab1 of Name-record
                  invoke CharacterArray "withLengthValue"
                         using     ls-Length
                                   Name-record
                         returning ls-string
                  invoke os-List "add"
                         using ls-string returning ls-string

             else  invoke os-List "add" using Name-record
          End-perform

        End Method "createScheduleCollection".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getLastNumber".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-number                    pic 9(03).
        Procedure division returning lnk-number.
          move ws-LastNumber to lnk-number
        End Method "getLastNumber".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getIndexFromKey".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        copy "\copylib\lnkObjVal.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ls==.
        *>------------------ lnkobjval.cpy------------------------------

        01  ls-ObjectValues.
           05 ls-Index                          pic x(4) comp-5.
           05 ls-RecLength                      pic x(4) comp-5.
           05 ls-Record.
              10 occurs 1 to 100
                 depending on ls-RecLength      pic x.
           05 ls-ObjectString                   object reference.

        *>--------------------------------------------------------------

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Key                       pic x(04).
        01 lnk-Index-Out                 pic x(4) comp-5.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-Key
                           returning lnk-Index-OUT.

         invoke super "getObjectFromKey"
                using lnk-Key returning ls-ObjectValues
         move ls-Index to lnk-Index-Out

        End Method "getIndexFromKey".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getKeyFromIndex".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        copy "\copylib\lnkObjVal.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==ls==.
        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-Index-In                  pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 lnk-Key                       pic x(04).

        Procedure Division using     lnk-Index-IN
                           returning lnk-Key.

         move spaces to lnk-key
         invoke super "getObjectFromIndex"
                using lnk-Index-In returning ls-ObjectValues
         move ls-record(PosKey of ws-Pos : 4 ) to lnk-key

        End Method "getKeyFromIndex".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "getScheduleNameObject".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------
        01 n                                 pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-length                         pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-length2                        pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-size                           pic x(4) comp-5.
        01 ls-string                         object reference.

        Linkage section.
        01 lnk-key                           pic x(04).
        01 lnk-Collection                    object reference.
        01 lnk-values.
           05 lnk-result                     pic 9(03).
           05 lnk-NameObject                 object reference.

        Procedure Division using     lnk-Key,
                                     lnk-Collection
                           returning lnk-values.

        move length of Name-record             to ls-length
        move length of Des-Name of Name-Record to ls-length2
        move 99                                to lnk-result

        invoke lnk-Collection "size" returning ls-size
        perform varying n from 1 by 1 until n > ls-size

           invoke lnk-Collection "at"
                  using n returning ls-string
           invoke ls-string "GetValueWithSize"
                  using ls-length returning Name-record

           if  lnk-key = Des-Code of Name-record
               move zeroes to lnk-result
               set lnk-NameObject to ls-string
               EXIT PERFORM
           End-if

        End-perform

        if    lnk-result <> zeroes
              move "* Invalid Name *" to Des-Name of Name-Record
              invoke CharacterArray "withLengthValue"
                 using ls-length2, Des-Name of Name-record
                 returning lnk-NameObject
        End-if

        End Method "getScheduleNameObject".
        *>---------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "makeListRecord".
        *>------------------------------------------------------------

           Evaluate true
             when ByName
               move CORR ws-DesListRecord to Name-record

               if TypeTabbed
                   move x'09' to Tab1 of Name-record
                                 Tab2 of Name-record
               End-if

               move Name-record to ws-TempRecord

             when ByKey
               move CORR ws-DesListRecord to Key-record

               if TypeTabbed
                   move x'09' to Tab1 of Key-record
                                 Tab2 of Key-record
               End-if

               move Key-Record to ws-TempRecord

             when other
               move CORR ws-DesListRecord to Other-record

               if TypeTabbed
                   move x'09' to Tab1 of Other-record
                                 Tab2 of Other-record
               End-if

               move Other-Record to ws-TempRecord
           End-evaluate

        if   ( Des-Code of ws-DeslistRecord is numeric      ) and
             ( Des-Code of ws-DeslistRecord > ws-LastNumber )
             move Des-code of ws-DeslistRecord to ws-LastNumber
        End-if

        End Method "makeListRecord".
        *>----------------------------------------------------------
        Method-id. "newDictionaryRecord".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

        *>  ***** invoked from super (DesTable) by iteration

        Linkage section.
        copy "deslist.cpy" replacing ==(tag)== by ==lnk==.

        Procedure division using lnk-DesListRecord.

          Evaluate true
            when ByKeyOnly
              invoke super "addToDictionary"
                     using Des-Code
                           Des-Name(1:1)

            when ByKeyAndName
            when ByKeyAndData

              invoke super "addToDictionary"
                     using Des-Code
                           Des-Name

            when ByKeyAndOther
              invoke super "addToDictionary"
                     using Des-Code
                           Des-Other1

            when ByNameAndKey
              invoke super "addToDictionary"
                     using Des-Name
                           Des-Code

            when RmPointsDictionary
              invoke super "addToDictionary"
                     using Des-Other2
                           Des-Code

          End-evaluate

        End Method "newDictionaryRecord".
        *>-------------------------------------------------------------

        End OBJECT.
        End CLASS DescripsDBI.

*>-----------------------------------------------------------------------

**** SQL DES TABLE ( I use MS Access) :

This is the final piece and the bit directly applicable to creating 
Collections is method "makeCollection". Note I've used COBOL syntax 
"wrtie" and "rewrite" as method-names - the intention of that - in 
classes invoking the data either COBOL ISAMs or SQL Tables can invoke 
"write" "rewrite" and it is only the object ISAMfile or SQLtable that is 
changed.

       $set sql (dbman=ODBC)

        *>-----------------tabdes.cbl----------------------------------

        Class-id.          DescriptionsTable
